  gode: { 8: 60, 9: 80, 10: 120, 11: 180, 12: 240, 13: 360 },
  halveGode: { 8: 80, 9: 120, 10: 180, 11: 240, 12: 360, 13: 420 }
};
BASE.halve = BASE.gode;
const OVER = { almindelig: 5, gode: 10, halveGode: 20 };
OVER.halve = OVER.gode;
const UNDER = { almindelig: -10, gode: -20, halveGode: -40 };
UNDER.halve = UNDER.gode;
const SOL_PTS = {
  sol: { win1: 180, win2: 120, lose1: -180, lose2: -180 },
  rensol: { win1: 240, win2: 180, lose1: -240, lose2: -240 },
  bord: { win1: 360, win2: 240, lose1: -360, lose2: -360 }
};
const SOL_OPP = {
  sol: { win1: -60, win2: -120, lose1: 60, lose2: 120 },
  rensol: { win1: -80, win2: -180, lose1: 80, lose2: 180 },
  bord: { win1: -120, win2: -240, lose1: 120, lose2: 240 }
};
function roundUp10(n) {
  return Math.ceil(n / 10) * 10;
}
function variantKey(round) {
  if (round.gameType === "halve") return round.trump === "\u2663" ? "halveGode" : "halve";
  return round.gameType;
}
function calcRoundPoints(round) {
  var _a;
  const gt = GAME_TYPES.find((g) => g.id === round.gameType);
  if (!gt || !round.declarer) return null;
  if (gt.solType) {
    const coDeclarers = round.coDeclarers || [];
    const allDec = [round.declarer, ...coDeclarers];
    const opponents = PLAYERS.filter((p) => !allDec.includes(p));
    const numDec = allDec.length;
    const tbl = SOL_PTS[round.gameType];
    const oppTbl = SOL_OPP[round.gameType];
    if (!tbl) return null;
    const maxAllowed = round.gameType === "sol" ? 1 : 0;
    const solTaken = round.solTaken || {};
    const pts2 = {};
    PLAYERS.forEach((p) => pts2[p] = 0);
    if (numDec === 1) {
      const taken2 = solTaken[round.declarer];
      if (taken2 === void 0 || taken2 === "") return null;
      const ok = Number(taken2) <= maxAllowed;
      pts2[round.declarer] = ok ? tbl.win1 : tbl.lose1;
      opponents.forEach((p) => pts2[p] = ok ? oppTbl.win1 : oppTbl.lose1);
    } else {
      allDec.forEach((dec) => {
        const taken2 = solTaken[dec];
        if (taken2 === void 0 || taken2 === "") return;
        pts2[dec] = Number(taken2) <= maxAllowed ? tbl.win2 : tbl.lose2;
      });
      const results = allDec.map((dec) => {
        const t = solTaken[dec];
        return t === void 0 || t === "" ? null : Number(t) <= maxAllowed;
      });
      if (results.every((r) => r === true)) opponents.forEach((p) => pts2[p] = oppTbl.win2);
      else if (results.every((r) => r === false)) opponents.forEach((p) => pts2[p] = oppTbl.lose2);
      else opponents.forEach((p) => pts2[p] = 0);
    }
    return pts2;
  }
  const bid = parseInt(round.bid);
  const taken = parseInt(round.taken);
  if (isNaN(bid) || isNaN(taken) || bid < 8 || bid > 13) return null;
  const key = variantKey(round);
  const base = (_a = BASE[key]) == null ? void 0 : _a[bid];
  if (base === void 0) return null;
  const diff = taken - bid;
  let decPts;
  if (diff >= 0) {
    const extra = diff > 0 ? roundUp10(diff * OVER[key]) : 0;
    decPts = base + extra;
  } else {
    const short = bid - taken;
    decPts = -base - short * Math.abs(UNDER[key]);
  }
  const pts = {};
  PLAYERS.forEach((p) => pts[p] = 0);
  if (round.partner === "selv") {
    pts[round.declarer] = decPts * 2;
    PLAYERS.filter((p) => p !== round.declarer).forEach((p) => pts[p] = -decPts);
  } else if (round.partner) {
    pts[round.declarer] = decPts;
    pts[round.partner] = decPts;
    PLAYERS.filter((p) => p !== round.declarer && p !== round.partner).forEach((p) => pts[p] = -decPts);
  } else return null;
  return pts;
}
const SUPABASE_URL = "https://oqzgtqxwovagkzprycre.supabase.co";
const SUPABASE_KEY = "sb_publishable_k5G52_w4_s9DvAYsHwn18Q_Mg-67lVx";
const DB_ROW_ID = 1;
async function cloudLoad() {
  try {
    const res = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/sessions?id=eq.${DB_ROW_ID}&select=data`, {
      headers: { "apikey": SUPABASE_KEY, "Authorization": `Bearer ${SUPABASE_KEY}` }
    });
    const rows = await res.json();
    if (rows && rows.length > 0) return rows[0].data;
    return [];
  } catch (e) {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
      return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : [];
    } catch (e2) {
      return [];
    }
  }
}
async function cloudSave(data) {
  try {
    await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/sessions`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "apikey": SUPABASE_KEY,
        "Authorization": `Bearer ${SUPABASE_KEY}`,
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "Prefer": "resolution=merge-duplicates"
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ id: DB_ROW_ID, data, updated_at: (/* @__PURE__ */ new Date()).toISOString() })
    });
    localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(data));
  } catch (e) {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(data));
    } catch (e2) {
    }
  }
}
const initRound = () => ({
  id: Date.now() + Math.random(),
  gameType: null,
  declarer: null,
  partner: null,
  trump: null,
  bid: "",
  taken: "",
  solTaken: {},
  coDeclarers: [],
  points: { Peter: "", Bj\u00F8rn: "", Kirk: "", Wehner: "" },
  autoPoints: true,
  collapsed: false
});
function Modal({ title, message, confirmLabel = "OK", confirmColor = "#b5451b", onConfirm, onCancel }) {
  return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.modalOverlay }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.modalBox }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("h3", { style: S.modalTitle }, title), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("p", { style: S.modalMsg }, message), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.modalBtns }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("button", { style: S.modalCancel, onClick: onCancel }, "Annuller"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("button", { style: __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, S.modalConfirm), { background: confirmColor }), onClick: onConfirm }, confirmLabel))));
}
function parseExcelToSessions(workbook) {
  const sheetName = workbook.SheetNames.find((n) => /result|whist|aften|data/i.test(n)) || workbook.SheetNames[0];
  const ws = workbook.Sheets[sheetName];
  const rows = window.XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(ws, { defval: "" });
  if (!rows.length) return [];
  const colMap = {};
  const sample = rows[0];
  Object.keys(sample).forEach((k) => {
    const kl = k.toLowerCase().trim();
    PLAYERS.forEach((p) => {
      if (kl === p.toLowerCase() || kl.includes(p.toLowerCase())) colMap[p] = k;
    });
  });
  const dateCol = Object.keys(sample).find((k) => /dato|date|dag|aften/i.test(k));
  const sessions = [];
  rows.forEach((row, ri) => {
    const hasPoints = PLAYERS.some((p) => colMap[p] && row[colMap[p]] !== "" && !isNaN(Number(row[colMap[p]])));
    if (!hasPoints) return;
    let dateStr = dateCol ? String(row[dateCol]).trim() : "";
    if (!dateStr || dateStr === "0") dateStr = `Importeret r\xE6kke ${ri + 1}`;
    const points = {};
    PLAYERS.forEach((p) => {
      const raw = colMap[p] ? row[colMap[p]] : "";
      points[p] = raw !== "" && !isNaN(Number(raw)) ? String(Number(raw)) : "";
    });
    sessions.push({
      id: Date.now() + ri + Math.random(),
      date: dateStr,
      finished: true,
      imported: true,
      rounds: [__spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, initRound()), { id: Date.now() + ri + 0.5, gameType: "almindelig", points, autoPoints: false })]
    });
  });
  return sessions;
}
function calcSessionStats(rounds, roundPtsFn) {
  const typeCounts = {};
  GAME_TYPES.forEach((g) => typeCounts[g.id] = 0);
  const declarerCounts = {};
  PLAYERS.forEach((p) => declarerCounts[p] = 0);
  const declarerWins = {};
  PLAYERS.forEach((p) => declarerWins[p] = 0);
  let totalRounds = 0;
  rounds.forEach((r) => {
    if (!r.gameType || !r.declarer) return;
    typeCounts[r.gameType] = (typeCounts[r.gameType] || 0) + 1;
    declarerCounts[r.declarer] = (declarerCounts[r.declarer] || 0) + 1;
    totalRounds++;
    const pts = roundPtsFn(r);
    if (pts && pts[r.declarer] > 0) declarerWins[r.declarer]++;
  });
  return { typeCounts, declarerCounts, declarerWins, totalRounds };
}

  function startSession() {

    });
    const lastSeason = ((_a = existing[0]) == null ? void 0 : _a.season) || 11;

  function exportSessionToExcel(session, allSessions) {
    if (!window.XLSX) return;
    const XLSX = window.XLSX;
    const gameTypeLabel = (r) => {
      const bid = r.bid || "";
      const gt = r.gameType || "";
      const label = {
        "almindelig": "Alm",
        "gode": "Gode",
        "halve": "Halve",
        "sol": "Sol",
        "rensol": "Ren Sol",
        "bord": "Opl\xE6gger"
      }[gt] || gt;
      if (gt === "sol" || gt === "rensol" || gt === "bord") return label;
      if (gt === "halve" && r.trump === "\u2663") return bid ? `${bid} Halve Gode` : "Halve Gode";
      return bid ? `${bid} ${label}` : label;
    };
    const g\u00E5etHjem = (r) => {
      const pts = r.points || {};
      const dec = r.declarer;
      const part = r.partner;
      if (!dec) return "";
      const decPts = parseInt(pts[dec]) || 0;
      if (part && part !== "selv") {
        const partPts = parseInt(pts[part]) || 0;
        if (decPts > 0 && partPts > 0) return "Ja";
        if (decPts <= 0 && partPts <= 0) return "Nej";
        return "B\xE5de Og";
      }
      return decPts > 0 ? "Ja" : "Nej";
    };
    const allSorted = [...allSessions, __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, session), { finished: true })].sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.season && b.season) {
        if (a.season !== b.season) return a.season - b.season;
        return a.eveningNum - b.eveningNum;
      }
      return a.id - b.id;
    });
    const accTotals = { Bj\u00F8rn: 0, Kirk: 0, Peter: 0, Wehner: 0 };
    let roundNum = 0;
    const rows = [];
    for (const sess of allSorted) {
      for (const r of sess.rounds || []) {
        roundNum++;
        const pts = {};
        ["Bj\xF8rn", "Kirk", "Peter", "Wehner"].forEach((p) => {
          var _a;
          pts[p] = parseInt((_a = r.points) == null ? void 0 : _a[p]) || 0;
          accTotals[p] += pts[p];
        });
        const dato = sess.date && !sess.date.includes("S\xE6son") ? sess.date : "";
        rows.push([
          roundNum,
          null,
          dato || null,
          sess.season || null,
          sess.eveningNum || null,
          gameTypeLabel(r),
          r.declarer || null,
          r.partner === "selv" ? r.declarer : r.partner || null,
          g\u00E5etHjem(r),
          pts.Bj\u00F8rn,
          pts.Kirk,
          pts.Peter,
          pts.Wehner,
          accTotals.Bj\u00F8rn,
          accTotals.Kirk,
          accTotals.Peter,
          accTotals.Wehner
        ]);
      }
    }
    const header = [[" ", "Arena", "Dato", "S\xE6son", "Aften", "Melding", "Melder", "Makker", "G\xE5et Hjem", "Bj\xF8rn", "Kirk", "Peter", "Wehner", "Akk_Bj\xF8rn", "Akk_Kirk", "Akk_Peter", "Akk_Wehner"]];
    const ws2 = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([...header, ...rows]);
    ws2["!cols"] = [
      { wch: 6 },

    const wb2 = XLSX.utils.book_new();
    XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb2, ws2, "Samlet statistik");

  function finishSession() {

  function loadHistory() {
    const existingIds = new Set(sessions.map((s) => String(s.id)));
    const toAdd = HISTORICAL_DATA.filter((s) => !existingIds.has(String(s.id)));
    if (toAdd.length === 0) {
      setModal({ title: "Allerede importeret", message: "Historikken er allerede indl\xE6st.", confirmLabel: "OK", onConfirm: () => setModal(null) });
      return;
    }
    setModal({
      title: `Indl\xE6s ${toAdd.length} aftenener?`,
      message: `Indl\xE6ser ${toAdd.length} historiske kortaftenener fra dit Excel-ark.`,
      confirmLabel: "Indl\xE6s",
      confirmColor: "#2c7a4b",
      onConfirm: () => {
        const merged = [...sessions, ...toAdd].sort((a, b) => {
          if (a.season && b.season) {
            if (a.season !== b.season) return b.season - a.season;
            return b.eveningNum - a.eveningNum;
          }
          return b.id - a.id;
        });
        saveSessions(merged);
        setModal(null);
        setView("history");
      }
    });
  }
  function handleFileChange(e) {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    setImportStatus(null);
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = (ev) => {
      try {
        const wb = window.XLSX.read(new Uint8Array(ev.target.result), { type: "array" });
        const imported = parseExcelToSessions(wb);
        if (!imported.length) {
          setImportStatus({ error: "Ingen gyldige r\xE6kker fundet." });
          return;
        }
        setModal({
          title: `Importer ${imported.length} aftenener?`,
          message: `Fandt ${imported.length} r\xE6kker.`,
          confirmLabel: "Importer",
          confirmColor: "#2c7a4b",
          onConfirm: () => {
            saveSessions([...sessions, ...imported].sort((a, b) => b.id - a.id));
            setImportStatus({ ok: true, count: imported.length });
            setModal(null);
            setView("history");
          }
        });
      } catch (err) {
        setImportStatus({ error: "Fejl: " + err.message });
      }
    };
    reader.readAsArrayBuffer(file);
    e.target.value = "";
  }
  function roundPts(r) {
    if (r.autoPoints) {
      const auto = calcRoundPoints(r);
      if (auto) return auto;
    }
    const t = {};
    PLAYERS.forEach((p) => {
      const v = parseInt(r.points[p]);
      t[p] = isNaN(v) ? 0 : v;
    });
    return t;
  }
  function sessionTotals(sess) {
    const t = {};
    PLAYERS.forEach((p) => t[p] = 0);
    sess.rounds.forEach((r) => {
      const rp = roundPts(r);
      PLAYERS.forEach((p) => t[p] += rp[p] || 0);
    });
    return t;
  }
  const allTotals = () => {
    const t = {};
    PLAYERS.forEach((p) => t[p] = 0);
    sessions.forEach((s) => {
      const st = sessionTotals(s);
      PLAYERS.forEach((p) => t[p] += st[p]);
    });
    return t;
  };
  const rankings = () => {
    const t = allTotals();
    return PLAYERS.slice().sort((a, b) => t[b] - t[a]).map((p, i) => ({ name: p, total: t[p], rank: i + 1 }));

    const tot = totals[p];
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { key: p, style: S.totalChip }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: S.totalName }, p), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, S.totalPts), { color: tot > 0 ?   })), active.rounds.map((round, ri) => /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(

  return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.collapsedCard, onClick: onExpand }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: "10px", flex: 1, minWidth: 0 } }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: S.collRoundNum }, "R", roundIdx + 1), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: S.collGtBadge }, gt ? `${gt.emoji} ${gt.label}` : "\u2014"), round.declarer && /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: S.collDeclarer }, round.declarer, round.partner && round.partner !== "selv" ? ` & ${round.partner}` : round.partner === "selv" ? " (selv)" : "")), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: "6px" } }, pts && PLAYERS.map((p) => {
    const v = pts[p];
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { key: p, style: __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, S.collPtChip), { color: v > 0 ? "#2c7a4b" : v < 0 ? "#b5451b" : "#999", background: v > 0 ? "#f0f9f4" : v < 0 ? "#fdf0ee" : "#f5f5f5" }) }, p.slice(0, 2), " ", v > 0 ? "+" : "", v);
  }), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: S.expandHint }, "\u25BC"), canRemove && /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("button", { onClick: (e) => {

function SessionStatsPanel({ stats, rounds }) {
  const { typeCounts, declarerCounts, declarerWins, totalRounds } = stats;
  if (totalRounds === 0) return null;
  const activeTypes = GAME_TYPES.filter((g) => typeCounts[g.id] > 0);
  const maxCount = Math.max(...activeTypes.map((g) => typeCounts[g.id]), 1);
  return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statsPanel }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("p", { style: S.cardLabel }, "Aftenens statistik"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("p", { style: S.statSubhead }, "Spiltyper (", totalRounds, " runder)"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: "6px", marginBottom: "18px" } }, activeTypes.map((g) => /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { key: g.id, style: { display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: "10px" } }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: { width: "110px", fontSize: "13px", fontWeight: 600, color: "#444", flexShrink: 0 } }, g.emoji, " ", g.label), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { flex: 1, background: "#f0ece3", borderRadius: "4px", height: "18px", overflow: "hidden" } }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { width: `${typeCounts[g.id] / maxCount * 100}%`, height: "100%", background: "#1a1a2e", borderRadius: "4px", transition: "width .4s ease" } })), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: "13px", fontWeight: 700, color: "#1a1a2e", width: "24px", textAlign: "right" } }, typeCounts[g.id])))), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("p", { style: S.statSubhead }, "Meldinger per spiller"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", gap: "8px", flexWrap: "wrap", marginBottom: "18px" } }, PLAYERS.map((p) => {
    const c = declarerCounts[p] || 0;
    const w = declarerWins[p] || 0;
    const pct = c > 0 ? Math.round(w / c * 100) : 0;
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { key: p, style: S.statPlayerChip }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: S.statPlayerName }, p), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: S.statPlayerBig }, c), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: S.statPlayerSub }, "meldinger"), c > 0 && /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, S.statPlayerPct), { color: pct >= 50 ? "#2c7a4b" : "#b5451b" }) }, pct, "% hjem"));
  })), rounds.filter((r) => r.gameType && r.declarer).length > 0 && /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(React.Fragment, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("p", { style: S.statSubhead }, "Rundeoversigt"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: "4px" } }, rounds.filter((r) => r.gameType && r.declarer).map((r, i) => {
    const gt = GAME_TYPES.find((g) => g.id === r.gameType);
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { key: r.id, style: { display: "flex", gap: "8px", alignItems: "center", fontSize: "13px", color: "#555", padding: "5px 0", borderBottom: "1px solid #f5f0e8" } }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: { color: "#bbb", width: "20px", flexShrink: 0 } }, "#", i + 1), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: { width: "110px", flexShrink: 0 } }, gt ? `${gt.emoji} ${gt.label}` : "\u2014"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: { flex: 1 } }, r.declarer, r.partner && r.partner !== "selv" ? ` & ${r.partner}` : r.partner === "selv" ? function GlobalStats({ sessions, roundPtsFn }) {
  const allRounds = sessions.flatMap((s) => s.rounds).filter((r) => r.gameType && r.declarer);
  const total = allRounds.length;
  if (sessions.length === 0 || total === 0) return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.col }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("h2", { style: S.pageTitle }, "Statistik"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("p", { style: S.empty }, "Ingen data endnu. Spil en kortaften f\xF8rst!"));
  const totals = {};
  PLAYERS.forEach((p) => totals[p] = 0);
  sessions.forEach((s) => {
    s.rounds.forEach((r) => {
      const pts = roundPtsFn(r);
      PLAYERS.forEach((p) => {
        var _a;
        return totals[p] += pts ? (_a = pts[p]) != null ? _a : 0 : 0;
      });
    });
  });
  const ranked = PLAYERS.slice().sort((a, b) => totals[b] - totals[a]).map((p, i) => ({ name: p, total: totals[p], rank: i + 1 }));
  const medals = ["\u{1F947}", "\u{1F948}", "\u{1F949}", "4\uFE0F\u20E3"];
  const typeCounts = {};
  GAME_TYPES.forEach((g) => typeCounts[g.id] = 0);
  allRounds.forEach((r) => typeCounts[r.gameType] = (typeCounts[r.gameType] || 0) + 1);
  const maxType = Math.max(...Object.values(typeCounts), 1);
  const normName = (name) => {
    if (!name || name === "selv") return null;
    return PLAYERS.find((p) => p.toLowerCase() === name.toLowerCase()) || null;
  };
  const playerStats = {};
  PLAYERS.forEach((p) => playerStats[p] = { declared: 0, won: 0, partner: 0, totalPts: totals[p], bestPts: -Infinity, worstPts: Infinity });
  allRounds.forEach((r) => {
    const dec = normName(r.declarer);
    if (dec) {
      playerStats[dec].declared++;
      const pts = roundPtsFn(r);
      if (pts && pts[dec] > 0) playerStats[dec].won++;
      if (pts) {
        playerStats[dec].bestPts = Math.max(playerStats[dec].bestPts, pts[dec]);
        playerStats[dec].worstPts = Math.min(playerStats[dec].worstPts, pts[dec]);
      }
    }
    const part = normName(r.partner);
    if (part) playerStats[part].partner++;
  });
  const solRounds = allRounds.filter((r) => ["sol", "rensol", "bord"].includes(r.gameType));
  const solWins = solRounds.filter((r) => {
    const p = roundPtsFn(r);
    return p && p[normName(r.declarer)] > 0;
  }).length;
  const partnerPairs = {};
  allRounds.forEach((r) => {
    const dec = normName(r.declarer);
    const part = normName(r.partner);
    if (dec && part) {
      const key = [dec, part].sort().join(" & ");
      partnerPairs[key] = (partnerPairs[key] || 0) + 1;
    }
  });
  return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.col }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("h2", { style: S.pageTitle }, "Statistik"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("p", { style: S.pageSub }, sessions.length, " aftenener \xB7 ", total, " runder"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "grid", gridTemplateColumns: "repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr))", gap: "12px" } }, ranked.map((r, i) => {
    const ps = playerStats[r.name];
    const winPct = ps.declared > 0 ? Math.round(ps.won / ps.declared * 100) : 0;
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { key: r.name, style: __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, S.playerStatCard), { borderTop: `3px solid ${i === 0 ? "#f0b429" : i === 1 ? "#aaa" : i === 2 ? "#cd7f32" : "#ddd"}` }) }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: "10px", marginBottom: "12px" } }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: "28px" } }, medals[i]), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { fontWeight: 900, fontSize: "18px", fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif" } }, r.name), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: "11px", color: "#aaa", letterSpacing: "1px", textTransform: "uppercase" } }, "Plads ", r.rank)), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { marginLeft: "auto", textAlign: "right" } }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: "26px", fontWeight: 900, fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", color: r.total >= 0 ? "#2c7a4b" : "#b5451b" } }, r.total > 0 ? "+" : "", r.total), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: "11px", color: "#bbb" } }, "point"))), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "grid", gridTemplateColumns: "1fr 1fr", gap: "6px", borderTop: "1px solid #f0ece3", paddingTop: "10px" } }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statCell }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statCellBig }, ps.declared), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statCellLabel }, "meldinger")), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statCell }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, S.statCellBig), { color: winPct >= 50 ? "#2c7a4b" : "#b5451b" }) }, winPct, "%"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statCellLabel }, "hjem")), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statCell }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statCellBig }, ps.partner), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statCellLabel }, "som makker")), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statCell }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, S.statCellBig), { fontSize: "14px", color: "#2c7a4b" }) }, ps.bestPts > -Infinity ? "+" + ps.bestPts : "\u2014"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statCellLabel }, "bedste runde"))));
  })), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { style: S.statsPanel }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("p", { style: S.cardLabel }, "Fordeling af spiltyper"), GAME_TYPES.filter((g) => typeCounts[g.id] > 0).map((g) => {
    const pct = Math.round(typeCounts[g.id] / total * 100);

function OvertrickLabel({ taken, bid }) {
  if (taken === "" || bid === "") return null;
  const d = parseInt(taken) - parseInt(bid);
  if (isNaN(d)) return null;
  if (d > 0) return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, S.bidLabel2), { color: "#2c7a4b" }) }, "+", d, " overtrick", d > 1 ? "s" : "");
  if (d < 0) return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, S.bidLabel2), { color: "#b5451b" }) }, d, " stik for lidt");
  return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: __spreadProps(__spreadValues({}, S.bidLabel2), { color: "#2c7a4b" }) }, "Pr\xE6cis hjem \u2713");
}
function SolCheck({ val, maxAllowed }) {
  if (val === "" || val === void 0 || val === null) return null;
  const ok = Number(val) <= maxAllowed;
  return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: "18px" } }, ok ? "\u2705" : "\u274C");
}
